10. Таймер с обратным отсчётом

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <p>{{ timeLeft }} seconds</p>
    <button @click="startTimer">Start Timer</button>
    <button @click="stopTimer">Stop Timer</button>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      timeLeft: 60,
      timer: null,
    };
  },
  methods: {
    startTimer() {
      if (this.timer) return;
      this.timer = setInterval(() => {
        if (this.timeLeft > 0) {
          this.timeLeft--;
        } else {
          this.stopTimer();
        }
      }, 1000);
    },
    stopTimer() {
      clearInterval(this.timer);
      this.timer = null;
    },
  },
};
</script>

11. Форма регистрации

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="name" placeholder="Enter your name" />
    <input v-model="email" type="email" placeholder="Enter your email" />
    <input v-model="password" type="password" placeholder="Enter your password" />
    <button @click="register">Register</button>
    <p v-if="message">{{ message }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      name: "",
      email: "",
      password: "",
      message: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    register() {
      if (this.name && this.email && this.password) {
        this.message = "Registration successful!";
      } else {
        this.message = "All fields are required!";
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

12. Погода

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="city" placeholder="Enter city" />
    <button @click="getWeather">Get Weather</button>
    <div v-if="weather">
      <p>{{ weather.name }}: {{ weather.main.temp }}°C</p>
      <p>{{ weather.weather[0].description }}</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      city: "",
      weather: null,
    };
  },
  methods: {
    async getWeather() {
      const apiKey = "YOUR_API_KEY";
      const response = await fetch(
        `https://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?q=${this.city}&appid=${apiKey}&units=metric`
      );
      const data = await response.json();
      this.weather = data;
    },
  },
};
</script>

13. Обратная связь

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <textarea v-model="feedback" placeholder="Your feedback"></textarea>
    <button @click="submitFeedback">Submit</button>
    <p v-if="message">{{ message }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      feedback: "",
      message: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    submitFeedback() {
      if (this.feedback.trim()) {
        this.message = "Feedback submitted!";
        this.feedback = "";
      } else {
        this.message = "Please provide feedback.";
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

14. Генератор паролей

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <button @click="generatePassword">Generate Password</button>
    <p>{{ password }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      password: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    generatePassword() {
      const characters = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789!@#$%^&*()";
      let password = "";
      for (let i = 0; i < 12; i++) {
        password += characters.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length));
      }
      this.password = password;
    },
  },
};
</script>

15. Контактная форма

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="name" placeholder="Your Name" />
    <input v-model="email" type="email" placeholder="Your Email" />
    <textarea v-model="message" placeholder="Your Message"></textarea>
    <button @click="sendMessage">Send Message</button>
    <p v-if="confirmation">{{ confirmation }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      name: "",
      email: "",
      message: "",
      confirmation: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    sendMessage() {
      if (this.name && this.email && this.message) {
        this.confirmation = "Your message has been sent!";
        this.name = "";
        this.email = "";
        this.message = "";
      } else {
        this.confirmation = "All fields are required!";
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

16. Тема темной/светлой

vue
<template>
  <div :class="theme">
    <button @click="toggleTheme">Toggle Theme</button>
    <p>The current theme is {{ theme }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      theme: "light",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    toggleTheme() {
      this.theme = this.theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light";
    },
  },
};
</script>

<style>
.light {
  background-color: white;
  color: black;
}
.dark {
  background-color: black;
  color: white;
}
</style>

17. Галерея с фильтрацией

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="searchQuery" placeholder="Search images" />
    <div class="gallery">
      <img
        v-for="(image, index) in filteredImages"
        :key="index"
        :src="image.url"
        alt="Image"
      />
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      searchQuery: "",
      images: [
        { url: "https://placekitten.com/200/300" },
        { url: "https://placekitten.com/250/350" },
        { url: "https://placekitten.com/300/400" },
      ],
    };
  },
  computed: {
    filteredImages() {
      return this.images.filter(image =>
        image.url.toLowerCase().includes(this.searchQuery.toLowerCase())
      );
    },
  },
};
</script>

18. Слайдер изображений

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <img :src="images[currentImage]" />
    <button @click="prevImage">Previous</button>
    <button @click="nextImage">Next</button>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      currentImage: 0,
      images: [
        "https://placekitten.com/200/300",
        "https://placekitten.com/250/350",
        "https://placekitten.com/300/400",
      ],
    };
  },
  methods: {
    prevImage() {
      this.currentImage = (this.currentImage - 1 + this.images.length) % this.images.length;
    },
    nextImage() {
      this.currentImage = (this.currentImage + 1) % this.images.length;
    },
  },
};
</script>

19. Пагинация списка

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <ul>
      <li v-for="(item, index) in paginatedItems" :key="index">{{ item }}</li>
    </ul>
    <button @click="prevPage" :disabled="currentPage === 1">Previous</button>
    <button @click="nextPage" :disabled="currentPage === totalPages">Next</button>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      items: Array.from({ length: 100 }, (_, i) => `Item ${i + 1}`),
      currentPage: 1,
      itemsPerPage: 10,
    };
  },
  computed: {
    totalPages() {
      return Math.ceil(this.items.length / this.itemsPerPage);
    },
    paginatedItems() {
      const start = (this.currentPage - 1) * this.itemsPerPage;
      const end = start + this.itemsPerPage;
      return this.items.slice(start, end);
    },
  },
  methods: {
    prevPage() {
      if (this.currentPage > 1) this.currentPage--;
    },
    nextPage() {
      if (this.currentPage < this.totalPages) this.currentPage++;
    },
  },
};
</script>

20. Реализация поиска по списку

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="searchQuery" placeholder="Search" />
    <ul>
      <li v-for="(item, index) in filteredItems" :key="index">{{ item }}</li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      searchQuery: "",
      items: ["Apple", "Banana", "Cherry", "Date", "Grape", "Lemon", "Orange"],
    };
  },
  computed: {
    filteredItems() {
      return this.items.filter(item =>
        item.toLowerCase().includes(this.searchQuery.toLowerCase())
      );
    },
  },
};
</script>

21. Реализация чек-листа с отметкой выполненных задач

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <ul>
      <li v-for="(task, index) in tasks" :key="index">
        <input type="checkbox" v-model="task.completed" />
        <span :style="{ textDecoration: task.completed ? 'line-through' : 'none' }">
          {{ task.text }}
        </span>
      </li>
    </ul>
    <input v-model="newTask" placeholder="New task" />
    <button @click="addTask">Add Task</button>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      tasks: [
        { text: "Buy groceries", completed: false },
        { text: "Walk the dog", completed: true },
      ],
      newTask: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    addTask() {
      if (this.newTask.trim()) {
        this.tasks.push({ text: this.newTask, completed: false });
        this.newTask = "";
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

23. Динамическое создание компонентов

vue

  <div>
    <button @click="addComponent">Add Component</button>
    <div v-for="(component, index) in components" :key="index">
      <DynamicComponent :is="component" />
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      components: [],
    };
  },
  methods: {
    addComponent() {
      this.components.push("ChildComponent");
    },
  },
  components: {
    ChildComponent: {
      template: "<div>Dynamic Component!</div>",
    },
  },
};
</script>

24. Калькулятор

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input type="number" v-model.number="num1" />
    <select v-model="operator">
      <option value="+">+</option>
      <option value="-">-</option>
      <option value="*">*</option>
      <option value="/">/</option>
    </select>
    <input type="number" v-model.number="num2" />
    <button @click="calculate">=</button>
    <p>{{ result }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      num1: 0,
      num2: 0,
      operator: "+",
      result: null,
    };
  },
  methods: {
    calculate() {
      switch (this.operator) {
        case "+":
          this.result = this.num1 + this.num2;
          break;
        case "-":
          this.result = this.num1 - this.num2;
          break;
        case "*":
          this.result = this.num1 * this.num2;
          break;
        case "/":
          this.result = this.num2 !== 0 ? this.num1 / this.num2 : "Error: Division by zero";
          break;
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

</script>

    },
  },
};
</script>

28. Панель уведомлений

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <button @click="addNotification">Add Notification</button>
    <div v-for="(notification, index) in notifications" :key="index">
      {{ notification }}
      <button @click="removeNotification(index)">Dismiss</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      notifications: [],
    };
  },
  methods: {
    addNotification() {
      this.notifications.push(`Notification ${this.notifications.length + 1}`);
    },
    removeNotification(index) {
      this.notifications.splice(index, 1);
    },
  },
};
</script>

32. Поиск в таблице

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <input v-model="searchQuery" placeholder="Search by name" />
    <table border="1">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Name</th>
          <th>Age</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        <tr v-for="person in filteredPeople" :key="person.name">
          <td>{{ person.name }}</td>
          <td>{{ person.age }}</td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      searchQuery: "",
      people: [
        { name: "Alice", age: 25 },
        { name: "Bob", age: 30 },
        { name: "Charlie", age: 35 },
      ],
    };
  },
  computed: {
    filteredPeople() {
      return this.people.filter(person =>
        person.name.toLowerCase().includes(this.searchQuery.toLowerCase())
      );
    },
  },
};
</script>

33. Динамическая подгрузка данных

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <button @click="loadMore">Load More</button>
    <ul>
      <li v-for="item in visibleItems" :key="item.id">{{ item.text }}</li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      items: Array.from({ length: 20 }, (v, i) => ({ id: i, text: `Item ${i + 1}` })),
      visibleCount: 5,
    };
  },
  computed: {
    visibleItems() {
      return this.items.slice(0, this.visibleCount);
    },
  },
  methods: {
    loadMore() {
      this.visibleCount += 5;
    },
  },
};
</script>

34. Таймер обратного отсчета

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <p>Time left: {{ timeLeft }} seconds</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      timeLeft: 10,
    };
  },
  created() {
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      if (this.timeLeft > 0) {
        this.timeLeft--;
      } else {
        clearInterval(timer);
      }
    }, 1000);
  },
};
</script>

36. Управление избранными элементами

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <ul>
      <li
        v-for="(item, index) in items"
        :key="index"
        :class="{ favorite: favorites.includes(index) }"
        @click="toggleFavorite(index)"
      >
        {{ item }}
      </li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      items: ["Apple", "Banana", "Cherry", "Date"],
      favorites: [],
    };
  },
  methods: {
    toggleFavorite(index) {
      if (this.favorites.includes(index)) {
        this.favorites = this.favorites.filter(fav => fav !== index);
      } else {
        this.favorites.push(index);
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

<style>
.favorite {
  color: red;
  font-weight: bold;
}
</style>

37. Динамическое управление формой

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <button @click="addField">Add Field</button>
    <form>
      <div v-for="(field, index) in fields" :key="index">
        <input v-model="field.value" placeholder="Enter value" />
        <button type="button" @click="removeField(index)">Remove</button>
      </div>
    </form>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      fields: [],
    };
  },
  methods: {
    addField() {
      this.fields.push({ value: "" });
    },
    removeField(index) {
      this.fields.splice(index, 1);
    },
  },
};
</script>

38. Изменение темы сайта

vue
<template>
  <div :class="theme">
    <button @click="toggleTheme">Toggle Theme</button>
    <p>The current theme is: {{ theme }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      theme: "light",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    toggleTheme() {
      this.theme = this.theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light";
    },
  },
};
</script>

<style>
.light {
  background-color: white;
  color: black;
}
.dark {
  background-color: black;
  color: white;
}
</style>

39. Форма авторизации

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <form @submit.prevent="login">
      <input v-model="username" placeholder="Username" />
      <input v-model="password" type="password" placeholder="Password" />
      <button type="submit">Login</button>
    </form>
    <p v-if="message">{{ message }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      username: "",
      password: "",
      message: "",
    };
  },
  methods: {
    login() {
      if (this.username === "admin" && this.password === "1234") {
        this.message = "Login successful!";
      } else {
        this.message = "Invalid credentials.";
      }
    },
  },
};
</script>

40. Простой опросник

vue
<template>
  <div>
    <h3>What is your favorite color?</h3>
    <label v-for="(color, index) in colors" :key="index">
      <input type="radio" :value="color" v-model="selectedColor" />
      {{ color }}
    </label>
    <p>You selected: {{ selectedColor }}</p>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      colors: ["Red", "Blue", "Green"],
      selectedColor: "",
    };
  },
};
</script>

Эти примеры представляют собой задачи, охватывающие различные аспекты Vue.js, такие как работа с динамическими элементами, формами, состоянием и стилями.
